Do you think that you can not push arbitrary numbers on the stack?
No need to worry.

You can push -255 ~ 0  values within 3+24 characters.
You can push 0 ~ 10000 values within 3+40 characters.

You can push 0 at top of the stack with operand  ( 1  character ) '0'
You can push 1 at top of the stack with operands (3+0 characters) '00='
You can push 2 at top of the stack with operands ( +2 characters) '00="+'
You can push 3 at top of the stack with operands (  4 characters) '00=""++'

Also you can push negative values. -N is '00="(-N - 1)-'
ex.  3 is '00= ""++ '
    -2 is '00="""++-'

'(N)000=%-' is another way to push -N.
ex.  3 is '00=""++      '
    -3 is '00=""++000=%-'
